               <script type="text/javascript">
                jQuery(window).load(function() {
 
 						
 													jQuery('#flexslider-home_banner').flexslider({
 								namespace: 				"sw-flexslider-",
 																easing:					"jswing",
 																useCSS:					false,
 								directionNav: 			true,
 								controlNav:				false,
 								keyboard: 				true,
 								multipleKeyboard: 		true,
 								slideshow:				true,
 																startAt: 				0,
 																animationLoop:			true,
 								pauseOnAction: 			false,
 								pauseOnHover: 			false,
 								animation: 				"fade",
 								animationSpeed: 		600,
 								direction: 				"horizontal",
 								slideshowSpeed: 		7000,
 								randomize: 				false,
 								smoothHeight: 			false,
 								controlsContainer: 		".flex-nav-container",
 																																start: function(slider){
 																		jQuery('.sw-flexslider-container').removeClass('loading');
 									animateCaption_home_banner();
 									if (slider.slides.eq(0).find('iframe.youtube-autoplay-1').length) {
 										jQuery('#flexslider-home_banner').flexslider("pause");
 										setTimeout(function() {
 											playVideo_home_banner(jQuery('.youtube_1:not(.clone) iframe.youtube').attr('id'));
 										},2000);
 									}
 									if (slider.slides.eq(0).find('iframe.vimeo-autoplay-1').length) {
 										jQuery('#flexslider-home_banner').flexslider("pause");
 										setTimeout(function() {
 											$f(jQuery('.vimeo_1:not(.clone) iframe.vimeo').attr('id')).api('play');
 										},600);
 									}
 								},
 								before: function(slider) {
 																											resetCaption_home_banner();
 								},
 								after: function(slider) {
 																		animateCaption_home_banner();
 								},
 							});
 
 							/* remove loader bar when pause on action is active */
 							jQuery('.sw-flexslider-prev, .sw-flexslider-next, .sw-flexslider-control-nav, .sw-flexslider-control-paging').click(function(){
 															});
 
 						 // end if not carousel
 
 					}); // end window.load
 
 					/* JAVASCRIPT FUNCTIONS */
 
 					/* change slide on overlay mouseover */
 					
 					/* animate the captions or not */
 					function animateCaption_home_banner(){
 						jQuery("#flexslider-home_banner .slides .sw-flexslider-active-slide .slider-title").show();
 						jQuery("#flexslider-home_banner .slides .top-animated-caption").delay(200).animate({top:'0'}, 800);
 						jQuery("#flexslider-home_banner .slides .bottom-animated-caption").delay(200).animate({bottom:'0'}, 800);
 						jQuery("#flexslider-home_banner .slides .top-left-animated-caption, #flexslider-home_banner .slides .bottom-left-animated-caption").delay(200).animate({left:'0'}, 800);
 						jQuery("#flexslider-home_banner .slides .top-right-animated-caption, #flexslider-home_banner .slides .bottom-right-animated-caption").delay(200).animate({right:'0'}, 800);
 					}
 					function resetCaption_home_banner(){
 						jQuery("#flexslider-home_banner .slides .slider-title").hide();
 						jQuery("#flexslider-home_banner .slides .top-animated-caption").css({top: '-100%'});
 						jQuery("#flexslider-home_banner .slides .bottom-animated-caption").css({bottom: '-100%'});
 						jQuery("#flexslider-home_banner .slides .top-left-animated-caption, #flexslider-home_banner .slides .bottom-left-animated-caption").css({left: '-50%'});
 						jQuery("#flexslider-home_banner .slides .top-right-animated-caption, #flexslider-home_banner .slides .bottom-right-animated-caption").css({right: '-50%'});
 					}
 
 					/* animation functions for the loader bar */
 					function animateLoader_home_banner(varDuration){
 						jQuery('#flexslider-home_banner .loader').width('0%').animate({width: '100%'}, {easing: 'linear', duration: varDuration, queue: false, complete: function(){jQuery('#flexslider-home_banner .loader').width('0%');}});
 					}
 					function stopAnimateLoader_home_banner(timeDelay){
 						if (typeof(timeDelay) === "undefined") {
 							jQuery('#flexslider-home_banner .loader-gutter').delay(200).fadeOut();
 						} else {
 							jQuery('#flexslider-home_banner .loader-gutter').hide();
 						}
 					}
 					function resumeAnimateLoader_home_banner(){
 						jQuery('#flexslider-home_banner .loader-gutter, .loader').clearQueue();
 						animateLoader_home_banner(7000);
 						jQuery('#flexslider-home_banner .loader-gutter').delay(200).fadeIn();
 					}
 
 					/* pause loaderbar on hover when pauseonhover is true */
               </script>

                <div class="body-content-wrapper">
                 <div class="body-content">
                  <div class="page-title">
                   <h1>
                    Bradfords Building Supplies
                   </h1>
                  </div>
                  <div class="std">
                   <p style="text-align: left;">
                    It was way back in 1770 when Mr Bradford first opened his doors to West Country trades.
                   </p>
                   <p style="text-align: left;">
                    Fast forward 250 years and our passion and commitment to providing the best service to local business remains our priority.  With more than 50 branches across the South West, a great new website and a range of delivery options, we’re never too far away.
                   </p>
                   <p style="text-align: left;">
                    Whatever your trade, we're here to help you get the best job done.
                   </p>
                   <p style="text-align: left;">
                    For expert advice and everything you need under one roof; both online and in branch.
                   </p>
                   <h2 style="text-align: left;">
                    Bradfords. Trusted by Trades since 1770.
                   </h2>
                  </div>
                 </div>
